zinbryta contains daclizumab beta , a monoclonal antibody . this is a type of protein that attaches to a protein called myelin . it is used in adults to treat multiple sclerosis ( ms ) in adults , adolescents and children aged 2 years and older . therapy is based on the results of a two - year course of therapy followed by other treatments . inflammation destroys the protective sheath that protects the nerves in the central nervous system ( the brain ) and spinal cord . if you lose any of these parts of your body , it is called demyelinating , which can lead to the relapsing condition , repeated attacks ( relapses ), and symptoms of damage to your nerves . when these nerves are damaged , you should tell your doctor .
do not take zinbryta - if you have previously had a serious allergic reaction to daclizumab or any of the other ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before taking this medicine if : - you have liver problems . - your doctor will tell you how to take the medicine and how often to take it . tell your doctor or pharmacist if any of these apply to you . your doctor may decide to change your dose . this is because you may not be able to take any other autoimmune disorders . it is also important that you do not have any other medicines , such as herbal supplements , or any medicines or supplements that may cause liver side effects . these medicines are not recommended for use in children and adolescents . you should not take this medicine in children under the age of 18 years .

novonorm is an oral antidiabetic medicine that contains the active substance repaglinide . it works by stopping the pancreas from making enough insulin to control your blood sugar ( glucose ). type 2 diabetes is a disease in which your body does not make enough insulin . the sugar in your blood is stored in the blood and is absorbed by the body . this helps the body make better use of the insulin it produces . novonlorm is used for the treatment of type2 diabetes in adults , adolescents and children aged 2 years and older . treatment with exercise and weight reduction has been shown to reduce the amount of sugar that you can take with metformin , which is also used to treat diabetes .
do not take novonorm : - if you are allergic to repaglinide or any of the other ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before taking this medicine if : you have type 1 diabetes . your doctor will check the acid level in your blood ( diabetic ketoacidosis ). you have a severe liver disease . you are taking gemfibrozil , a medicine used to lower increased fat levels 47 you have liver problems . if any of these apply to you , tell your doctor or pharmacist before taking novonom , as this may affect your ability to drive or use machinery . it is also important that you inform your doctor as soon as possible if your doctor tells you that you have moderate liver disease ( see section 4 ). your doctor may decide to reduce the dose of no
always take this medicine exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor or pharmacist if you are not sure . the recommended dose is one 0 . 5 mg tablet once a day . swallow the tablet whole with a glass of water . you can take novonorm with or without food . your doctor will tell you how many tablets to take and how long you should take them . do not take more than 30 tablets . take the tablet at least 4 hours before or at least 30 minutes before or 16 hours after your meal . if your blood sugar is too low or you have a hypo , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . it is important that you tell your doctor as soon as possible if it is too high or too low . this will help to control your diabetes , and your doctor may decide to stop your treatment with this medicine .
like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . hypoglycaemia is a common side effect that may affect more than 1 in 10 people . if you have a hypo in section , your doctor may decide to reduce the dose of novonorm to a lower dose , which may be more appropriate or less appropriate for you . your doctor will tell you how many doses to take , how often to take and when to stop taking the medicine and the frequency of the side effects listed below , as well as the frequency cannot be estimated from the available data , and how often you should take the medicine . you should tell your doctor as soon as possible if any of these side effects get serious , or if your doctor decides that you may need to stop the medicine or stop taking it . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet .

pumarix is a vaccine for adults aged 18 years and older . it is used to prevent pandemic flu ( influenza ) in adults , adolescents , and children aged 10 years and over . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you are given the vaccine . your doctor will decide on the type of vaccine that is right for you . you will also be given a different type of flu vaccine , which will help protect you from the flu . all vaccines will be given to children and adolescents under the age of 18 years who are vaccinated .
pumarix will not be given to you if you have ever had a sudden life - threatening allergic reaction to any of the ingredients of this vaccine ( listed in section 6 ): chicken protein , ovalbumin , formaldehyde and sodium deoxycholate . signs of an allergic reaction include itchy skin rash , shortness of breath and swelling of the face or tongue . warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you are given the vaccine . medical treatment may be necessary . a possible allergic reaction has been reported in patients receiving this vaccine 33 . your doctor or nurse will monitor you closely for any allergic reaction . you will be given this vaccine at least 6 weeks after the last dose . it is important that you follow all the instructions for the use of the vaccine carefully . children and adolescents this vaccine is not recommended for children under 6 years of age .
pumarix will be given to you by a doctor or nurse who is experienced in administering a similar h5n1 as03 vaccine to a child under 18 years of age . the recommended dose is one ml of vaccine for adults and children aged 3 - 9 years , aged 3 months to 10 - 17 years . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , nurse or nurse before you are given this vaccine . it is given as an injection into a muscle in your upper arm . do not give this vaccine to children below the age of 18 .

remicade contains the active substance infliximab , which belongs to a group of medicines called ' tnf blockers '. it is used to treat the following inflammatory diseases : rheumatoid arthritis , psoriatic arthritis ( ankylosing spondylitis , bechterew 's disease ) and in adults , adolescents , and children 6 years of age and older , who are not able to tolerate the effects of crohn' s disease or ulcerative colitis . remikade works by blocking its action . it works by reducing the amount of protein called tumour necrosis factor alpha a type of protein that is involved in the inflammatory response .

remicade is used to treat rheumatoid arthritis in adults , adolescents and children 3 years of age and older , based on body weight . psoriatic arthritis , ankylosing spondylitis ( bechterew ' s disease ) in adults and children of all ages , including children and adolescents aged 5 years and above . the recommended dose is one 5 mg infusion of body weight per day . your doctor will prescribe the right dose for you , depending on your ability to tolerate the medicine . it is given as an infusion ( drip ) over 2 hours in the veins of your upper arm . after the third treatment , your doctor may decide to increase the dose if you are not sure . you will be given one or more infusions over a period of at least one week .
like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . the majority of side effects are mild to moderate . serious side effects may occur during treatment . tell your doctor straight away if you notice any of the following side effects during your treatment with remicade : - an allergic reaction , such as swelling of your face , lips , mouth or throat , difficulty in swallowing or breathing , skin rash , hives or swelling of the hands , feet or ankles . these reactions may be serious and may be life - threatening . if any of these reactions occur , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . this includes any possible allergic reaction not listed in this leaflet . you can also report allergic side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information

mvasi contains the active substance bevacizumab , which is a humanised monoclonal antibody . it works by binding to a protein called human vascular endothelial growth factor ( vegf ), which is produced by the immune system in the body to fight infection , cancer , and other forms of infection . mvai binds to the protein that controls the growth of cells in the lymph vessels of the body . by binding to this protein , it stimulates blood vessels to produce more oxygen , allowing the tumour to grow . this helps to stop tumour growth in the blood vessels and the nutrients that are needed to provide oxygen to the cells . the active ingredient is : a medicine for the treatment of advanced cancer in the large bowel ( colon ) that has spread to other parts of the colon .

do not take tecartus - if you are allergic to any of the ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). if your doctor thinks you may be allergic , ask your doctor for advice . warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before taking the medicine . your doctor will check the number of white blood cells in your blood ( lymphodepleting chemotherapy ). children and adolescents 3 years of age and older are more likely to have a low number of these cells . autologous use is not recommended . tests and checks will be performed on the lungs , heart , kidney , blood pressure , infection , inflammation , or your cancer . if any of these apply to you , tell your doctor or nurse . you may also be at risk of developing graft - against - host disease or you have had a transplant .
tecartus will be given to you by a doctor or nurse who is experienced in the use of your own white blood cells . your cells will be injected into a catheter placed in a vein . a procedure call leukapheresis will be performed to remove the cells from your blood . this will take about 3 to 6 weeks , depending on how well your blood is circulating . you will be monitored by your doctor , nurse or nurse . the number of your white blood cell count will be checked every 2 to 3 weeks . medicines will also be prescribed to you if you are being treated for lymphodepleting chemotherapy , your doctor will decide how long your treatment will last . it is important that you do not have to take other medicines to prevent infusion reactions , such as fever , during treatment with these other medicines . please see section 4 .

xadago is a medicine that contains the active substance safinamide , which increases the levels of dopamine in the brain . this helps the brain to work more efficiently . it is used to treat patients with parkinson ' s disease whose symptoms are sudden switches in the way you are able to move . if you have difficulties moving , you should contact your doctor immediately . the medicine is also used in combination with levodopa and other medicines used for the treatment of parkinsons disease .

zytiga is a medicine that contains the active substance abiraterone acetate . it is used to treat prostate cancer that has spread to other parts of the body , and to reduce the amount of testosterone in your blood . zymiga is used in adults , adolescents and children whose prostate cancer is not being treated with hormone therapy ( a treatment that lowers testosterone ( androgen deprivation therapy ). it is also used in combination with another medicine , prednisone , or prediabetes , to treat high blood pressure , which causes your body to build up more testosterone , thereby reducing fluid retention . your doctor will check how well your blood is working .

kinzalmono belongs to a group of medicines called angiotensin ii receptor antagonists . it works by blocking the activity of the enzyme , which causes the body ' s natural defences to cause its own blood vessels to narrow . this causes your blood pressure to rise . by blocking this activity , the blood vessels relax and the blood pressure rises , and so it is easier for you to keep up with your life - style . the active substance in this medicine is a type of essential hypertension ( high blood pressure ) in adults and children . if this happens , it can damage blood vessels in several organs and can lead to heart attack , heart or kidney failure , stroke , blindness .

enyglid is an oral antidiabetic medicine that contains the active substance repaglinide . it works by helping your pancreas make more insulin , which lowers your blood sugar ( glucose ). type 2 diabetes is a disease in which your body does not make enough insulin to control the level of sugar in your blood . the sugar is released into the blood by the body , and the body makes more of the insulin it produces . your doctor will work out the best way to reduce the amount of sugar that your body can make . you will also be given the medicine in combination with metformin to control diabetes . this medicine is also used to treat diabetes in adults and adolescents .

nplate ' s active ingredient is romiplostim , a protein that helps to prevent low platelet counts in patients with immune ( idiopathic ) thrombocytopenic purpura ( itp ). itp is a disease that affects the number of platelets in your body . platelets are important because they help to prevent blood clots from forming . if you have very lowplatelet counts , you may experience bruising and serious bleeding . it is used in children and adolescents aged 1 year and older who have had their spleen removed . chronic itp occurs when you have previously been treated with corticosteroids or immunoglobulins . what n plate looks like and contents of the pack of tablets is white to off - white , round , oval - shaped tablets .
do not take nplate : - if you are allergic to romiplostim or any of the other ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before taking n plate if : you have been allergic to other medicines that contain escherichia coli ( e . coli ). if any of these apply to you , ask your doctor for advice . you should tell your doctor as soon as possible in case you have a low blood platelet count ( thrombocytopenia ). your doctor may decide to increase your dose . your platelet counts should be checked regularly to check for blood clots . it is important that you keep a close watchful eye on the possibility of a build - up of red blood cells . this is especially important if this happens .
always use nplate exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor or pharmacist if you are not sure . the recommended dose is 1 to 17 mg / kg of body weight . your doctor will tell you how many doses you should take and how often you should use them . n plate is given as an injection under the skin ( subcutaneous ). it is given once a day . you will be given 1 ml / m2 of your blood platelet counts . it is important that you take regular blood samples to check that your platelets are working properly . this will help your platelet count and how well your blood is working . how much to inject yourself , your doctor may decide to increase or decrease the number of platelets in your blood . for more information , see the section " instructions for use " below . children and adolescents from 1 month to 17 years of age

zoledronic acid hospira contains a substance called bisphosphonates . this substance belongs to a group of medicines called ' sulfate '. it is used in adults to treat bone change , bone complications ( e . g . fractures ) and bone metastases ( cancer at the primary site of the bone ). it is also used to treat calcium in adults who have a tumour . tumours in the bone can increase the amount of calcium in your bone , leading to tumour - induced hypercalcaemia .

like all medicines , zoledronic acid hospira can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . the following side effects have been reported : very common ( may affect more than 1 in 10 people ): - severe kidney impairment ( seen in blood tests ) - low level of calcium in the blood ( seen uncommonly in 1 in 100 people ). - pain in the mouth , teeth and / or jaw , swelling or non - healing sores inside the mouth ( jaw discharge ), numbness , feeling of heaviness or loosening of a tooth , bone damage in the jaw ( osteonecrosis ). tell your doctor immediately if you notice any of these symptoms . talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet .
keep out of the sight and reach of children . do not use zoledronic acid hospira after the expiry date which is stated on the carton and blister after exp . store in a refrigerator ( 2 8 ). do not freeze . keep the bottle tightly closed in order to protect from light .

filgrastim ratiopharm contains the active substance filgra stim . filgrarstim is a protein produced in the body by escherichia coli . it belongs to a group of proteins called granulocytes , which are produced by the bone marrow . this helps the body produce new blood cells . if you have more blood cells called white cells , your body will start to produce more white cells which help your body fight infection . when you have a low number of white blood cells in your body , you will not get enough of them , but it is important that you get the best results for your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you start to get a high number of them in the first few weeks of chemotherapy , bone mmarrow transplantation or severe chronic neutropenia ( dna ) in adults and adolescents .

always take this medicine exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor or pharmacist if you are not sure . how much to take the recommended dose is one tablet a day . the tablets should be taken by mouth every 12 hours . take riluzole zentiva with or without food . your doctor will tell you how many tablets to take . do not take a double dose to make up for a forgotten dose . if your doctor tells you to take more tablets than you should , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nearest hospital emergency department immediately . it is important that you take the tablets at the same time each day , with food , drink and water . this will help to protect the environment .

emgality contains the active substance galcanezumab . it is a medicine that blocks the activity of the calcitonin gene ( cgrp ). it is used to treat migraine in adults , adolescents and children aged 4 years and older . the frequency of migraines in adults and children is controlled by a doctor who is experienced in the treatment of migraine headache and who are able to improve your quality of life .
do not take emgality : - if you are allergic to galcanezumab or any of the other ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before taking this medicine if : you have a serious cardiovascular disease . - you are pregnant or breast - feeding . this medicine is not recommended for patients with serious cardiovascular diseases . allergic reactions emmgality can cause serious allergic reactions ( see section 4 ). these reactions are usually mild to moderate . these reactions can affect up to 40 people . you should tell your doctor or nurse immediately if any of these reactions occur . such signs may be associated with side effects . children and adolescents this medicine should not be used in infants and children below the age of 18 years . other medicines and this medicine are not recommended in this age group . pregnancy and

daklinza contains the active ingredient daclatasvir . it is used to treat adults with hepatitis c , an infectious disease that affects the liver and spreads to other parts of the body . this medicine works by stopping the growth of a type of virus called ' h1n1 '. h2n1 is a virus that causes your body to produce more of the virus in your body , making it harder for the virus to grow . your doctor will test your blood for signs of h3n1 and tell you what you need to do before you start to get better . if you have any further questions on the use of this medicine , ask your doctor , pharmacist or nurse .

proquad is a vaccine against measles , mumps , rubella and chickenpox ( varicella ) viruses . when the vaccine is given , antibodies are produced to help protect you from the diseases that affect you . if you are a person who is not vaccinated , your child ' s immune system may not be able to fight these viruses properly . the antibodies help the immune system to fight diseases caused by these viruses , which can be life - threatening , and prevent them from spreading . you should not be given the vaccine more than 12 months after the first dose . your doctor will decide how long you should continue to give the vaccine . it is important that you follow the instructions for national vaccination 9 months after your child has been given national vaccination .

proquad is injected into a muscle , usually under the skin , in the upper thigh or upper arm area . injections are given to the muscle in the lower limb and upper arm areas , at the injection site . if you have a blood clotting disorder or low levels of platelets , your doctor will decide if the vaccine is suitable for you . the vaccine will be injected under your skin to reduce the risk of bleeding from the muscle . your doctor or nurse will check if it is safe for you to inject it directly into the blood vessel . when it is given to you by injection , it is important that you follow your doctor ' s instructions on how to inject the vaccine .
like all vaccines , this vaccine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . allergic reactions , such as hives , may occur . these reactions may cause difficulty in breathing or swallowing . if you have an allergic reaction , tell your doctor immediately . other side effects of proquad may affect up to 1 in 100 people . seizures and a fever may occur very rarely . uncommon ( may affect more than 1 in 1 , 000 people ) bronchiolitis , which can cause difficulty breathing , cough or unsteadiness with walking . the following side effects have been reported in patients treated in the past , including : very common : may affect as many as 1 in 10 people , injection site complaints . reporting of side effects in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by

rivastigmine hexal is a type of medicine called cholinesterase inhibitors . it is used to treat adults with alzheimer ' s dementia , dementia or parkinson 's disease . certain nerve cells die in the brain , and the neurotransmitter acetylcholine ( a substance produced by nerve cells ) does not work as well as it should . by inhibiting the enzymes that break down the amino acid in the body , it reduces the levels of the enzyme that make it easier for nerve cells to work properly . in this case , the effect is reduced by reducing the number of nerve cells in your brain . this helps to prevent nerve cells from working properly and reduce the symptoms of dementia .

the recommended dose of pemetrexed hospira is 500 mg / m2 of your body ' s surface area , based on your height and weight . this body surface area will be measured by your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . treatment will depend on your blood cell counts and on how well you respond to treatment . you will be given a dose that is right for you . the dose you will receive is one infusion ( 9 ml ). the other ingredients are cisplatin and water for infusion into your veins , lasting 30 minutes . if you have any further questions on the use of this product , ask your doctor or pharmacist .

bexsero is a meningococcal group b vaccine , which is given to children and adolescents aged 2 years and older . it is given by a doctor who is experienced in the treatment of disease caused by the neisseriameningitidis group - b bacteria . these bacteria cause infections called meningitis ( inflammation of the brain and spinal cord ) and sepsis ( blood poisoning ). the vaccine is used to prevent the disease from spreading .

nitisinone mdk contains the active substance nitric acid . this medicine is used to treat a rare disease called hereditary tyrosinemia ( a type of disease that affects more than 1 in 10 people ). this disease affects your body ' s ability to make the amino acid tirosine ( amino acids ) that is produced in the body . by reducing the amount of this medicine that your body produces , your body breaks down the harmful substances that are present in this medicine . it is important that you take this medicine exactly as your doctor has told you . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . your doctor will tell you what you need to do to make sure that you are getting the right kind of medicine that will help your body break down the bad substances .

orgalutran contains the active substance ganirelix . it belongs to a group of medicines called anti - gonadotrophin . gnrh is a type of hormone produced by the body ' s own body - derived cells called follicle stimulating hormone ( fsh ). gsh regulates the release of gonadotropins , which help to stimulate the growth , development , and reproduction of eggs in the ovaries . these eggs are produced in small round sacs called " egg cells " in the egg cells . this helps to release the mature egg cells and help to produce eggs in women , especially in women who are not able to reproduce themselves . in vitro fertilisation ( ivf ) and other methods have been used to achieve similar results .
do not take orgalutran if : you are allergic to ganirelix or any of the other ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). you are hypersensitive to gonadotrophin releasing hormone ( gnrh ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor or pharmacist before taking this medicine if you have : a moderate or severe kidney or liver disease . you are pregnant or breast - feeding . if any of these apply to you , tell your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . your doctor will monitor you closely before and during treatment . allergic reactions may occur in patients with an active allergic condition . additional monitoring and treatment may be necessary if allergic reactions occur in generalised , such as hives ( urticaria ), swelling of the face , lips tongue and / or throat , difficulty in breathing or swallowing ( angioedema

onbrez breezhaler contains the active substance indacaterol , which belongs to a group of medicines called bronchodilators . it works by relaxing the muscles that attach to the walls of the small air passages in the lungs . this makes breathing easier for people with breathing difficulties who have a lung disease called chronic obstructive pulmonary disease ( copd ). copd is a condition in which the muscles in your breathing are not working properly . your doctor will tell you how to use this medicine to relax the muscles of your lungs to make breathing easier .

rapiscan belongs to a group of medicines called ' coronary vasodilators '. it works by blocking the flow of blood through the heart arteries , which increases heart rate , and relaxes the muscles in your heart . rapiscan is used to perform a heart scan ( ' myocardial perfusion imaging '). the scan contains a radioactive substance called a ' radiopharmaceutical ' . these images are taken using a treadmill to work out how well your heart is working . after a scan , you will be given a small amount of radio pharmaceutical product injected into your body through a vein . it is important that you follow the instructions of your doctor .
do not use rapiscan - if you have a slow heart rate or high degree heart block ( sinus node disease ). if your doctor has prescribed a pacemaker for chest pain ( unstable angina ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you start treatment . low blood pressure ( hypotension ), heart failure , are allergic to regadenoson or any of the other ingredients of the medicine ( listed in section 6 ). children and adolescents : if any of these apply to you , tell your doctor as soon as possible if : you have recently had a serious heart problem , such as a heart attack , or you have abnormal heart rhythms . your doctor will tell you how often your heart beat is very fast or uneven . if this applies to you or your child ' s doctor will advise you when to stop treatment with 
rapiscan will be given to you by a doctor who is experienced in the treatment of your heart and blood pressure . it will be injected into a vein using 400 micrograms of a 5 ml solution . the injection will take 5 to 10 minutes depending on your weight . you will receive an injection of sodium chloride 9 mg , 9 mg or 5 mg a radioactive substance ( radiopharmaceutical ). your doctor will check your heart rate , blood pressure and the time of the injection . your doctor may decide to increase or decrease your dose if you need to have a dose that is right for you . if this happens , you will be monitored by your doctor , nurse or nurse . this is to make sure that your doctor has given you the right dose , depending on how well your heart is working and how well you are able to control blood pressure with the

viagra contains the active substance sildenafil , which belongs to a group of medicines called phosphodiesterase type 5 ( pde5 ) inhibitors . it works by blocking the activity of a protein in the blood vessels in the penis . this helps to keep your penis in order . viagra is used to help you get an erection if you are sexually stimulated . what is viagra used for viagra is a treatment for erectile dysfunction ( impotence ), a condition in which you cannot get , or keep , a re - errect penis suitable for sexual activity .
do not take viagra - if you are allergic to sildenafil or any of the other ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before taking viagra if : you are taking medicines containing nitrates , which can cause a dangerous fall in your blood pressure . these medicines are used to treat angina pectoris ( " chest pain "). the medicines are given to you by nitric oxide donors . you may be given amyl . riociguat . your doctor may prescribe this drug to treat pulmonary arterial hypertension ( high blood pressure in the lungs ). you are also at risk of chronic thromboembolic pulmonary hypertension , a condition that can lead to a build - up of blood clots ( pde ). 
always take this medicine exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor or pharmacist if you are not sure . the recommended dose is one 50 mg tablet of viagra a day . you can take viagra film - coated tablets or viagra orodispersible tablets with or without food . swallow the tablets whole with a glass of water . viagra is for oral use only . it is not recommended that you take viagra if your erection is not clear or you are sexually stimulated . your doctor will tell you how long you should take it . if it is more than one hour before you start taking viagra , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . do not take more viagra than you should unless your doctor tells you otherwise . this is because it may take longer than usual for the first time . taking viagra may cause an increase in side effects , which may be fatal
like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . talk to your doctor or pharmacist if you notice any of the side effects not listed in this leaflet . you may need to stop taking viagra and seek medical help immediately . the following side effects have been reported with viagra : an allergic reaction ( may affect up to 1 in 100 people ). symptoms may include sudden wheeziness , difficulty in breathing , dizziness or swelling of the eyelids , face , lips or throat . chest pains may occur when you are in a semi - sitting position . your doctor may prescribe nitrates to relieve your chest pain . prolonged and sometimes painful erections are uncommon . very common : may affect more than 1 in 1 , 000 people . a woman may have a slight increase in the number of men having an er

what palforzia contains the active substance is 0 . 5 mg / ml . each capsule contains 1 , 10 or 20 mg of powder . the other ingredients are microcrystalline cellulose , colloidal anhydrous silica ( e421 ), magnesium stearate and 100 mg oral powder in capsules . this powder is a clear , colourless , open - coated tablet . it is supplied in a glass vial containing colloidal ammonia , and a syringe , with or without lidded sachet . - the powder is white to off - white , opalescent , beige oral powder and initial dose escalation ( see section 3 , 13 , 5 , single - dose blisters ) are available . not all pack sizes may be marketed 
zerene contains the active substance benzodiazepine , which belongs to a group of medicinal products called hypnotic actions . it is used to treat sleeping problems after treatment . treatment should be stopped if you have problems sleeping .
do not take zerene - if you have hypersensitivity ( an allergy ) to zaleplon , or any of the other ingredients of the medicine ( listed in section 6 ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before taking the medicine , as zeene sleep apnoea syndrome is used to treat short periods of short durations of severe kidney or liver problems . myasthenia gravis is very weak , tired muscles , severe breathing , chest problems in patients under 18 years of age and older . your doctor will tell you about undesirable effects . you should not take any medicine or any medicines that may cause physical dependence during treatment . withdrawal symptoms may include headaches , muscle pain , extreme anxiety or tension . if any of these apply to you , tell your doctor or pharmacist straight away . children and adolescents zer
always take zerene exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor or pharmacist if you are not sure . how much to take the recommended dose is 10 mg once a day . your doctor will tell you how many capsules to take and how often to take them . take the capsules with food and drink . do not take more than your doctor tells you to take . you may experience difficulty falling asleep . people over the age of 65 years have mild to moderate liver problems . if your dose is less than 5 mg once daily , your doctor may decide to reduce your dose to 5 mg twice daily . the capsule may become cloudy or cloudy . this may be a sign of an overdose . becoming increasingly drowsy , you may be in a coma . talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse straight away if this happens .
like all medicines , zerene can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . talk to your doctor or pharmacist if you notice any other changes in your health . the frequency of the side effects listed below is based on the following : 36 common : may affect up to 1 in 10 people , may affect more than 1 in 100 people . uncommon : will affect 1 to 10 people in 1 , 000 people if not treated , will be monitored by a doctor or a nurse . not known : frequency cannot be estimated from the available data . other side effects may include : drowsiness , memory difficulties , sensations like tingling in the extremities . reporting of side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the
what zerene contains the active substance is zaleplon . each tablet contains 5 mg . the other ingredients are microcrystalline cellulose , pregelatinised starch , silicon dioxide ( e171 ), sodium lauryl sulphate , magnesium stearate , lactose monohydrate , indigo carmine , titanium dioxide , gelatin , titanium dioxide , red iron oxide , yellow iron oxide and black iron oxide (e172 ) in the tablet shellac , lecithin , simethicone . - the colourless tablets are white to off - white , oval - shaped tablets , engraved with " s - 13050 " on one side and " z " on the other side . not all pack sizes may be marketed .
